                 Netflix Recommendations
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 We all have Netflix. Let's recommend the stuff we enjoy to others so they can enjoy it too. What we love, is thoughtful considered reviews of Netflix movies/shows that you love, that will inspire your fellow members to watch it too. Please, put a bit of effort in and bear in mind you’re posting to almost a million people from all over the world. It would be really helpful to include the country or region where you’re viewing, because content does vary due to different licensing agreements. Unfortunately we have to limit posts on popular shows, to avoid spamming the group with multiple identical posts. We also decline posts that breach the rules (please check the rules), thanks!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 ANIME
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Rules 1 Be Kind and Courteous We're in this together to create a welcoming environment. Treat members and their values with respect. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. Do not disrupt group through your actions. 2 Zero Tolerance for Edgelords and Trolls Make sure everyone feels safe. Attempting to be edgy/trollish and subsequently spiteful, mean-spirited, or in any way insulting means your automatic consent to deletion from group. 3 Keep Content within Limits Do not post content that contains personal insults, discrimination, explicitly sexual content (including jokes), gore/violence, religion, politics, gender targeting, or advocacy of harmful behaviour. 4 Keep Discussions and Criticism Constructive By posting one's creative effort, they open it to both praise and criticism. However, criticism and comments that are deliberately hostile, rude, or insulting are not worthwhile and shall be deleted. 5 Keep Content Relevant Group allows fans to share their love for anime, comics, videogames, and everything related to geek culture. Let's keep it that way. If it's not related, it doesn't belong here. 6 Mark Spoilers Efficiently Mark plot sensitive posts as [SPOILER] and do not post screenshots or manga panels in your main post if they are part of the spoiler. Add them in the comment section if required. 7 No Promotions or Spam Give more to this group than you take. Self-promotion, spam and irrelevant links aren't allowed. Do not post links to other pages, groups or events. 8 Contact us for Reports, Questions, and Concerns
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Actors, Filmmakers, &amp; Job Postings!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 WHAT CAN BE POSTED TO THE WALL: Jobs and ONLY Jobs on the Wall! Acceptable Job Postings are: Film (feature, short, etc...) TV / Web Series or Pilots, Commercials, and Plays. Note: this Facebook group is primarily intended for the American, European, and Australian film making community, jobs outside these regions need to have enough compensation to at least cover travel and housing for these filmmakers. Once submitted allow about 24 hours for the job to be approved and posted, although this is usually much faster. Unacceptable postings are anything else! (This includes reality TV jobs and acting workshops.) Posting spam jobs will have you blocked and banned without a second chance. WHEN POSTING A JOB FOLLOW THIS FORMAT: TITLE &amp; TYPE: Feature, Pilot, Play, Short, Commercial, etc... CASTING: Gender, Age-Range, etc... and/or CREW CALL: Cinematographer, Sound Mixer, etc... LOCATION: City, State, Country (Do not say Starbucks on 7th!) COMPENSATION (clearly state: paying, non-paying, etc...) CONTACT (must include your email)! TIME(s): submission deadline, audition &amp; production time-frames Then below: ANYTHING ELSE! union status, requirements, links, etc... * Note: If the dates are firm and the job is paying $50/day or more, you are qualified to make your Job Posting an Event, therefore it will show up on the Wall like all the other Job Postings, but it will also show up on the event calendar.) ** Further note: There are 6 required lines. Put each item on it's own line and do not double space the lines! HOW TO PROMOTE YOURSELF: Upload your HEADSHOTS to PHOTOS put them in an ALBUM with your name and occupation as the Title and your info, contacts, and links as the Description. Upload your DEMO REELS to PHOTOS also. And upload your RESUMES to FILES! Make sure your File Name includes your name and your field of work i.e.: John-Doe_Actor.pdf NO CROWDFUNDING OR FINANCING: Posting about crowd funding, even posting for executive producers or producers to find you money is prohibited. Posting for money may cause you to be you blocked and banned without a second chance. NO BEGGING FOR LIKES GENERAL RULES: All posts must be in English albeit you may include a translation (in the same post below the English text). WARNING: Even though this group is moderated, it does not mean that anything on this group is accurate. Moderation is mostly an attempt to keep posters to follow the posting standards. The users of this group are responsible for all its content and all their interactions. The group is not and will not be liable for anything said or done by its users. FINAL NOTE: If you figure out a way to get your own unacceptable jobs or self promotions on the wall… (No I'm not going to tell you how to do it…) But if you figure it out and do it, you will be blocked and banned without a second chance. 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>

Memes such as insulting DBZ characters shall not be accepted in this group. 8.) If you are sharing contents from your private profiles, make sure the posts are in PUBLIC mode. 9.) Anyone who disrespects the admins' wishes shall be banned without a warning. 10.) This group will not be receiving posts during weekends. 11.)                  👉👉📌 GROUP RULES 📌 👈👈 WELCOME TWD FANS! To make this group the best that it can be, we have a few fundamental rules all members are required to follow: 📌 TO REPORT A COMMENT: To tag a comment, click the three dots (…) to the right of the person comment. Click “report to admin” 📌 YOU WILL SEE SPOILERS 👉This is a spoiler group, you will see spoilers. 👉The members in this group come from all time zones, therefore, spoilers will be posted as they are approved. 👉IF you don’t want to see the spoilers, please skip the post. 📌 CURSING IS NOT ALLOWED 👉If you are caught using curse words about a character, a member, or an actor, you will be MUTED for 24 hours. 👉If you are caught doing it again, you will be removed from the group. 📌 ACTOR BASHING IS NOT ALLOWED 👉If you are caught bashing an actor, you will be removed from the group 👉If you have issues upon removal, please contact the admin managers 📌 NO CHARACTER BASHING 👉You can discuss storylines, but badmouthing specific characters is not allowed. 👉If you are caught, you will be MUTED for 24 hours. 👉If you are caught doing it again, you will be removed from the group. 📌 NON-TWD DISCUSSIONS 👉We encourage you to make friends but if you find yourself discussing nonTWD related topics, please take elsewhere. Non-TWD related topics include: POLITICS, RELIGION, DAY-TO-DAY LIFE OUTSIDE TWD 👉If you are caught engaging in nonTWD discussions, you will be MUTED for 24 hours. 👉If you are caught consistently engaging in nonTWD talk in the group, you will be removed. 📌 ABSOLUTELY NO TROLLING OR BULLYING 👉Any harassing and/or bullying behavior towards another member will result in an immediate ban. 👉This includes correcting spelling/grammar, name-calling, body shaming, profile stalking, homophobic comments, racist comments, using slurs, calling someone a troll. 👉Grammar policing other members on a consistent basis 📌 ABSOLUTELY NO ADVERTISING OF ANY KIND 👉There is absolutely no advertising of any kind. 👉No links of any kind for any sales are allowed here. 👉No live events or streams 📌 WATCH PARTIES INVITES ARE NOT ALLOWED 👉While we encourage everyone to make friends, inviting members to join in watch parties are not allowed 📌 If you have questions or concerns, feel free to contact the admin manager Mary McBride or Jeanne Worth.

If you are posting casting calls please limit your posts to one time - and try to add a photo or flyer and make them look pretty! Any posts outside of reality TV casting calls will be removed and you will be banned from the group. We do not post for talk shows or acting roles. First post for any given show is free! Have a casting call that wants the most attention? Get pinned to the top of the calls for $25/week. Email KMossCasting@gmail.com for more info and availability. Need to post more than once for the same show? $10 for each additional post. 
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Movie Set Memes
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Movie Set Memes! Your virtual destination for the silly things you see or experience during production whether it be on set, during, or post! Content posted here should be relevant to working behind the scenes in film, tv, and commercials. We have a few rules below to make sure the experience is positive for everyone. 1. No self-promotion. This is not a place to advertise your passion project. 2. NO DOXING (google it). Harassment of any kind will result in a permanent ban. This includes going out of the group and attacking individuals on their personal facebook in reaction to something that gave birth on MSM. 3. No political discussion or trolling politics. Neutral memes with political figures like “Not Bad Obama” is fine if it's relevant but absolutely no arguing politics or using the group to make strong political statements. It never ends well online. 4. No posts/comments that promote sexual assault, sexual harassment, racism, etc. 5. No dissing on actual production companies or crew members because you had a bad experience with them. There are other groups for that. Movie Set Memes is not your personal army for justice—Witch-hunts are strictly forbidden. 6. Film Students are welcome! However don't say anything you may regret. Remember that your peers and professionals are on here and anything you say here CAN ACTUALLY affect your career. 7. TMZ type posts like actor drama or posts about upcoming blockbusters won’t be approved—Golden rule is if you post it, will someone who doesn’t work in the industry understand it? If the answer is “yes,” then it probably shouldn’t be posted... 8. Misusin' a meme? That’s a paddlin’... Your post doesn't have to be a meme, per se, however if you decide to use a popular image macro like Kermit drinking tea--please use it appropriately. If you're unsure, visit www.knowyourmeme.com . We welcome all forms of humor relating to the film production industry including meta jokes. 9. Don't waste the admins' time asking if "it's ok” to post something. Just post it and if it doesn't get approved, then it probably was too irrelevant or breaking some of these rules. Don't block admin. 10. Re-posts are allowed if they are presently relevant. It’s ok to post someone else’s meme or share a post from another group so long as you're not purposely promoting another group or page for your own personal gain. 11. Do not block admins. They are very sensitive. Have Fun! 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The rules are simple All post must include this information or it will not be approved. All post must have pictures of the product. NO STOCK PHOTOS When you are posting a mix of cosplays and clothing items. Please note this is a cosplay selling group so if your post is not at least 75% cosplay related, It will not be approved. Corsets/binders, Kimonos, and other traditional wear are okay. For selling... *Character name and series* Size/Measurements: Includes: Condition: Price: Images. If you are posting multiple cosplays, please make them all into 1-3 post. Everyone is now limited to 3 active post until this is resolved. Ex: Multiple full cosplays(series) ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~ WTB/ISO (Want To Buy or In Search Of Budget : Characters or series Size/Measurements: Location: Images: ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~ WTT (Want To Trade) Characters/items you have Character/items would want Characters/items you will not accept. Size: Location: Images. Ex. WTT I have multiple league of legends cosplays for (w.e characters.) Looking for any character from destiny or overwatch! Not interested in dva or soldier 76. Bam. You get approved and just add a photo of the cosplays you have with the measurements listed ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~ Post with clothing, figurines, random accessories etc will not be approved unless it is a prop or piece to a character. Ex. LOL Star guardian plushies. Or school bows for uniforms. Prop weapons. Etc . . . . . . If you cannot follow these steps for your post, I'm sorry but I will not be approved If you have any questions please message admins directly All transactions should be through paypals goods and services. Seller cannot expect buyer to pay the paypal fee. If a buyer says to do it through bank transfer or Family and Friends option, Decline and report! If you have any issues with a seller/buyer, contact the Admins immediately~

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 United Filmmakers Association
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Please check 'Info' tab for links to international UFA chapters. The United Filmmakers Association is dedicated to the encouragement of growth in global local film making opportunities through networking, collaboration, team building, action and empowerment. UFA supports these efforts by providing monthly networking sessions, online community forums, monthly and annual showcasing opportunities, connection to finance and distribution options as well as our online think tank to help fine tune projects. Each of our members is challenged to pay forward this help to the next wave of filmmakers by collaborating and advising fellow members and volunteering their guidance with our Youth Mentorship Foundation. We are Producers, Directors, Directors of Photography, Talent Agents, Managers, Wardrobe Designers, Prop Masters, Make-up Artists, Writers, Actors, Performers, Sound Specialists, Editors, Distributors, Stage Managers, Location Scouts, Casting Professionals, Still Photographers, Storyboard Artists, Animators, Special Effects Artists, Crew of all types as well as all those that aspire to these creative positions and we are UNITED in our call to action. If you have the will and the willingness to rise to our challenge, to collaborate and to pay forward, we invite you to join us. We are the UFA and we dare the creatives of world to be the force that envisions and helps manifest a better tomorrow for all. The United Filmmakers Association; creatives helping creative create… for a better world! 
                </div>
               </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Freelance Film Crew- Los Angeles
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is intended for freelance film professionals. Here we can ask questions of each other, network, look for jobs and hire crew. IT IS NOT, however a platform for you to spam about rental houses, or make daily posts about crowdfunds or spam about press for your completed project. Please do that on your own pages. If you have a crowdfund, you are permitted no more than twice a month or so. IN ADDITION, self promotion posts are not permitted, as they add a ton of clutter, and thereby the actual JOB POSTS get buried and people don't see them, and real opportunities are missed. We ask that you respect each other and pay for the services you require at group minimum or higher rates. We, like many of you grew tired of copy, credit, meal, posts on craigslist, other sites, and other Facebook groups. So, we therefore require than no gig be posted for less than $275 for a 12 hour day. If the day irs shorter, the group still mandates a $275/day minimum. If the day is longer, the rate should go up accordingly. In addition to our rate minimums, it must be clarified that these minimums DO NOT include and CANNOT include gear rental, kit fees, or materials fees. Such fees must be in addition to the labor rate. So, be sure to bear that in mind when posting. You have two options. One, you can post a set fee for gear, in addition to whatever labor rate you post. Two, you can post that you understand such fees are an extra cost and said fees can be negotiated privately. Finally, we may one exception to the rate minimum rules. We set a separate minimum, $210/12 hour day, for PAs. If more than 12 hours, you have to offer more. FINALLY. Because there is so much commotion whenever rates are not listed in a post, the following is the new policy. You cannot simply state "negotiable." Instead, you must acknowledge in writing, in your post, that the rate is negotiable, but will be no less than $275/12 hours. ALSO, it is illegal to post seeking a specific ethnicity, age, gender or someone of preferred sexual orientation. Any favoritism shown in this regard, no matter how minor, will get your post removed. Depending upon the situation, it may get you removed from the group. PLEASE no diatribe posts. In the case of violation, REPORT the post to ADMIN, and even tag myself, or another admin, like Cricket or KB. If we catch a post that does not conform to the labor rate minimum policies and fee policies, it will removed. If your post violates labor/discrimination law, it will be removed, and you may be removed along with it. People asking to join the page with obviously fake names/accounts will be rejected. There are three questions to answer. Finally, if you violate rules, there may be a PM sent assuming we believe the violation is an accident, but remember, we are busy, and it a courtesy, not a requirement. If it is felt the violation was made in spite of rules, you will be immediately removed permanently from the group. 
                </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Podcast Community
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group has three rules. 1. Play nice! Civil discussion and even respectful disagreement are encouraged but slander, name calling, snide mean spirited or condescending comments are not acceptable behavior. You will get a warning and continued negative behaviour will result in a temporary or permanent ban. 2. No question is a dumb question - If you use an acronym please define it and/or give a link to where people can get more info on it. Same goes for terms newbies might not be familiar with. 3. No self promotion - Introduce yourself when you join and give name or and/or url of your podcast but this is not the place to post "hey check out the episode I just posted" Get your own page/group for that. Happy Podcasting ~Megan Enloe Above is the simple version and is all you really need to read. A few people have asked me to expand on and explain the rules. So here is the extended version: 1. Podcasters are a fantastic community. This group went for months with “Play Nice” just being a given. Sadly that changed in September of 2012 and this rule had to be added. It turns out that a couple of people making snide condescending comments results in a handful of people making more snide condescending comments taking the opposing view. The rest of the community either goes silent because they don’t want to be on the receiving end of the negative comments or they simply leave the community all together. Trolls and any troll like behavior is banned in this group. If you have a problem with that you can take your troll arse out of my group. 2. Most Saturday mornings I can be found in Costa Mesa, CA attending Social Media Masterminds of Orange County. 30-50 people get together and discuss all things social and New Media. Yes, that many people drag themselves out of bed on a Saturday because the group is that useful. One of the reasons it is so good is that no question is a dumb question and the discussion is kept open to all levels of tech, social and New Media knowledge. Even when the discussion gets complicated the moderator insists that acronyms and uncommon terms are defined. The moderator makes sure people in the room feel ssafe. This group is a safe place to make comments and ask questions. If you have a problem with this, please see expanded notes on rule 1. 3. I realise the podcast or blog post you just put up is the best thing since sliced bread and EVERYBODY will want to know about it....but not everyone will agree with you. Since everyone in the group creates content of some kind this group would be a constant stream of the content we are creating if I didn’t have this rule in place. If you think your content, podcast, blog post etc. is useful to the group then run it past a few people in the group. If they are willing to put their reputation on the line and post it then it’s no longer self promotion. Regarding conferences, expos and award shows; This group was created, in part because I attended an event with a lot of other podcasters and didn’t realize we were all there together until the end of the conference. I had missed the opportunity to socialize with my fellow podcasters and went looking for a place online where podcasters would congregate and I could find out who would be attending events that are of interest to podcasters. When I could not find such a group I created this one. Expect to see promotion of Parsec Awards, Podcast Awards, Dragon*Con, Balticon, New Media Expo and any other event that has a strong podcasting track. It’s part of the reason this group was created. I would be happy to have representatives of the above Cons and award shows do an occasional post in this group because they are the original and best source of information about their event. Please run it by me first if you represent such an event just so we can all agree your event would be of interest to a large percentage of the community. This part gets a bit dicey for me because in September of 2012 I became an employee of New Media Expo. So I asked the group how much you all wanted to hear from me regarding my day job. The response was that major announcements are welcome as long as I don’t pester you with constant small updates. So when you see a post from me that promotes NMX (New Media Expo) please know that I have cleared this with the community and I have people who will keep me accountable if I post about NMX or the Podcast Awards too often. If you have a problem with this, please see expanded notes on rule 1. Happy Podcasting ~Megan Enloe
                </div>

                 The group created for Paul Walker fans. Also supporting Reach Out Worldwide org. Which is created to help others. About PAUL. Paul William Walker IV[3] (September 12, 1973[4] – November 30, 2013) was an American actor and philanthropist best known for his role as Brian O'Conner in The Fast and the Furious franchise. Walker began his career as a child actor during the 1970s and 1980s, but first gained recognition in the early 1990s after appearing in the television soap opera The Young and the Restless. He soon transitioned into film, and received praise in 1999 for his performances in the teen films She's All That and Varsity Blues, which helped kickstart his career. Walker then gained international fame after starring in The Fast and the Furious.

Any inappropriate content will be deleted immediately, and if there are multiple attempts to post inappropriate content you will be blocked from the Group without warning. Inappropriate content includes: - Revealing photos - Violent images - Images of a sexual nature 2. No bashing or bulling of other members. Anyone found doing so will be removed. 3. This is a CCS fan group so please let your post reflect that. Only CCS related content is allowed on our group. 4. No advertising of other groups or fan pages will be permitted unless it is given the "OK" by the admins. Your post will be removed if not previously approved, if you join the group and just come in and promote your page or group, you will be automatically removed. 5. Do not block admins. If any one of us is not able to participate in your threads or view your posts, you will be automatically removed from the group. 6. If you are found spamming with advertisements for items that are not CCS related, not only will you be removed but also your account reported to Facebook as fake. 7. DO NOT POST OR SHARE Chapter Spoilers before the official release date! Make sure you check with the official release date of the chapter before posting or sharing in this group. 8. Please do not spam the group! If you have more than one image to share with the group, please do it on the one post. If you continuously post separate images multiple times a day, you will be muted permanently. 9. This is not a page for promoting sales for yourself. We have a business thread available for promoting your products that you can share. If you try to post sales posts outside the thread it will be deleted. 10. This an international CCS fan group so make sure your post is written/translated in English. Post that are shared and written from another language will not be approved by us. 11. When sharing fan art from other artists, please include credits to the artist. Please remember that once content has been released it is permitted to share information about the new release. If you are unable to enjoy the new content when it has been released and don't want to see any spoilers, please unfollow the page until you have been able to enjoy the content yourself. It is your responsibility to ensure you're not exposed to the spoilers. Just follow these rules and have fun. If you have any ideas on how to improve and keep the group interesting, please feel free to suggest them to the admins. You will be given credit if your idea is implemented. Admin Staff x

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Podcast Movement Community - For Podcasters
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a place for people who are podcasters, looking to become a podcaster, or who are members of the podcasting industry! We have a few rules: 1. No Spam. No Self Promotion: We do not allow personal links to your podcast, website, Facebook page, Facebook group, Instagram, Twitter, organization, etc. We also do not allow image artwork / logos with your branding. You may not create a post that asks members of the group to post their links. The only exceptions to this rule is to either get advanced permission from the admin team if your post is truly beneficial to the community. You may post your links or artwork whenever the admin team allows this in a dedicated post within the group. Then, you may post in the comments only. 2. No Live Video Streaming / Pre-recorded Video unless approved by admins in advance. 3. No selling. No affiliate links. This means you may not resell your used microphone or attempt to sell your Podcast Movement registration, etc. 4. No Interview Requests. You may not use the group to seek opportunities to be interviewed. 5. Please be courteous. Do not make comments that are condescending, disrespectful, or rude to other members. Please be kind and gracious, especially with newer podcasters and their questions. We’ve seen some people making fun or just being unkind. Our focus is to keep the overall culture of the group positive and supportive. 6. Phrases: Our group does not allow the following phrases: ”Ok, Go!” or ”Am I right?”. We will not go and you are not right. 7. New Members: Please introduce yourself in the comments for the weekly introduction posts shared by the admin team. You may include your links in the comments of this approved post. 8. Community; We have a collaborative spirit and synergistic community. You may seek to help each other, but this should be done through asking questions, answering questions and encouraging each other. 9. Review Swaps are not allowed. We do not support, endorse or allow ratings &amp; review swaps. You can seek this type of opportunity in other podcast FB groups. 10. Use the Search: Before you ask a question in the group, please consider using the search feature to see if your question has already been addressed in the thousands of existing posts already.

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Are you looking to appear as a guest on a podcast or looking to find guests for a podcast you host? Are you ready to establish real relationships and collaborations with others? If you answered ‘yes’ to both of these questions, you are in the right place! We would love for you to join our Podcast Guest Collaboration Community that allows you to genuinely connect with others to find podcast guests for your podcast and/or to find podcasts to be a guest on. Other platforms (virtual summits, YouTube videos, etc.) are welcome too. **In order to expedite and highly increase your likelihood of approval, please answer all entry questions. Requesting to join this group means that you agree to the group rules (see below) and Terms of Use (click header image above) and are here to provide value in all your responses and collaborations.** What to expect here: &gt; Share and respond to #beaguest or #findaguest requests &gt; Opportunity to promote your podcast on Tuesdays in designated thread &gt; Opportunity to promote one social media handle on Fridays in designated thread &gt; Community support and encouragement &gt; Opportunity to join an exclusive community (Podcast Collab Club) to uplevel your collaborations Check out all the benefits of the Podcast Collab Club at: https://www.thepodcastcollaborative.com/podcast-collab-club/ Hope you can join us. The more the merrier! Please contact admin (Sarah Penner) if you have any concerns regarding members following these rules. I welcome your help in making sure this quality group runs smoothly and is of value to all members. Thanks! This group is operated by The Podcast Collaborative. By joining this group you are agreeing to the Group Rules and Terms of Use that you can find by clicking the header image above. We reserve the right to remove any member at our discretion. The information in this group is provided as general information and is not advice.                  Dragon Ball Fans Universe 7 (DBFU7)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello all! Welcome to DBFU7. In order for us to enjoy to the fullest we need to set guidelines where all members need to comply. I do not own any copyright or franchise of Dragon Ball. All images, videos, or art related to DB belong to Akira Toriyama and TOEI Animation, Inc. We, DBFU7, are a global community (multiethnic, social, economic, faith, etc). We share one thing in common: our love and passion for a fictional character or characters from the DB franchise. This group was created so we can share the things we love the most about our favorite characters: pics, videos, memes, theories, drawings, etc. We have noticed that some members want to use this group to promote their own platforms; well, we’d like to help you as long as you ask permission to do so, tag an admin or moderator, but remember: DBFU7 reserve the right to accept or deny your request. You can expect the admins and moderators being very courteous towards the community and we expect you do likewise to one another. There will be zero tolerance for racism, I’m warning you right now, if we (team dbfu7), found a member making racial slurs he will be eliminated (HAKAI) in the spot. DBFU7 has NO space for bigots of any kind. Spoilers have their place as long as you give us a warning you’re sharing spoilers. We will not allow spoilers at the time the episode is playing, all comments, images, reviews or videos will be played or allowed 24 hrs. after the episode has aired. This group IS NOT friendly of cyberbullies, porn, spam, political and/or religious views, ‘if you’re a true fan’, Goku vs Super Man, Anime vs Comics, ‘like my page/group/channel type’, Repeated posts will get deleted, not giving credit to artist or translator, claiming is your doing, will get you banned. We strongly encourage you to be as creative and original as possible, let’s make it fun, let’s make it enjoyable. Thank you for being part of an awesome group.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Date A Live's LN Translation
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is created to share updates, spoilers, and sometimes, translations of the LN series, Date A Live Group Rules: 1- Always respect each other in the comment section. This group was created to translate and read the Date A Live series, as well as sharing any interesting news, or spoilers. If you find yourself disagreeing with someone, settle the matter through private message. Attacks, or dismissive behavior shall not be tolerated. 2- Don't spam. Spamming, or uploading any type of content (unless it is official artwork) depicting nudity, use of drugs, rude language, or suggestive themes, will be deleted, and the person responsible shall be removed from the group. 3- Warn before uploading spoilers. While sharing new info regarding the plot is interesting and encouraged, we must respect those who don't feel the need to know things ahead of time. Any content that could be considered a spoiler should have a CLEAR and NOTICEABLE warning first to alert users about the content, followed by a minimum of FIVE blank lines to ensure obscurity. 4- Re-uploading archives. Unless the archive is taken down, no member will re-upload ANY file, be it an image, or text. If you want to re-upload something, ask one of the admins first for approval. If you want to know the location of a certain archive, check this group's archives under files. 5-Translation Updates: Refrain from pestering translators with questions of updates. The decision lies solely on the translator's discretion. Especially, complaints about not being up to date when a new volume is announced or released. By all means, DO NOT POST ANY QUESTIONS REGARDING UPDATES. 6. Uploading Content Versus discussions should be posted in another group. These discussions promote lengthy arguments over subjective opinions, and the discussions stray away from DAL as the main focus. Files uploaded in epub or PDF format must focus solely on Date A Live. Though collaboration efforts are still more than welcome if you can find someone willing to help with translating.
                </div>

                 AnimeCosmo
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Anime sometimes called Japanimation, is hand-drawn and computer animation originating from Japan. The term anime is derived from the English word animation, and in Japan is used to refer to all forms of animated media. Outside Japan, the term refers specifically to animation from Japan or to a Japanese-disseminated animation style often characterized by colorful graphics, vibrant characters and fantastical themes. This culturally abstract approach to the word's meaning may open the possibility of anime produced in countries other than Japan. Follow our page: https://www.facebook.com/AnimeCosmo
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Back To The Future Forever
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Created for all Back to the future fans around the world! Back to the Future is a 1985 science fiction adventure film directed by Robert Zemeckis, co-written by Bob Gale and produced by Steven Spielberg. The film stars Michael J. Fox as Marty McFly, as well as Christopher Lloyd, Crispin Glover, Lea Thompson and Thomas F. Wilson. Back to the Future tells the story of Marty McFly, a teenager who is accidentally sent back in time from 1985 to 1955. He meets his parents in high school, accidentally attracting his mother's romantic interest. Marty must repair the damage to history by causing his parents to fall in love, while finding a way to return to 1985. Zemeckis and Gale wrote the script after Gale mused upon whether he would have befriended his father if they attended school together. Various film studios rejected the script until the box office success of Zemeckis' Romancing the Stone, and the project was set up at Universal Pictures with Spielberg as executive producer. Eric Stoltz was originally cast as Marty McFly, but during filming he and the filmmakers decided he was miscast: the subsequent recasting meant the crew had to race through reshoots and post-production to complete the film for its July 3, 1985 release date. When released, it became the most successful film of the year, grossing more than $380 million worldwide and receiving critical acclaim. It won the Hugo Award for Best Dramatic Presentation and the Saturn Award for Best Science Fiction Film, and also earned Academy Award, BAFTA and Golden Globe nominations. Ronald Reagan even quoted the film in the 1986 State of the Union Address, and in 2007, the Library of Congress selected it for preservation in the National Film Registry. It marked the beginning of a franchise, with Back to the Future Part II and Back to the Future Part III released back-to-back in 1989 and 1990, as well as an animated series and theme park ride. 
                </div>
               </div>

So please refrain from swearing. Also please don't post inappropriate images/videos. 03 - Be kind and courteous We're all in this together to create a welcoming environment. Let's treat everyone with respect. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. Insulting Mods will result in removal from the group. 04 - No hate speech or bullying Make sure everyone feels safe. Bullying of any kind isn't allowed, and Degrading comments about things such as politics, race, religion, culture, sexual orientation, gender or identity will not be tolerated. 05 - Duplicates To keep the group focused and organized, we will remove duplicate posts, especially links. Priority will be given to our own stories from What's On Disney Plus. Please try using "Search" first. 06 - No Piracy/Sharing/Selling Accounts/Passwords No posts or comments discussing the sharing, trading, selling, leasing, or subleasing of Disney+ accounts. No discussion or promotion of piracy or illegal streams 07 - Spoilers Avoid posting spoilers in your original posts. Spoilers may be revealed in the comments of the discussion, but please make it obvious so readers can avoid ie #SPOILER# 08 - No Low Quality Posts If a post is deemed low quality. It may not be approved. This may include short text posts, bad quality images or unnecessary links 09 - No Spam Do not private message, post or comment any spam, affiliate links, referral codes, or advertise any product or service or yourself. This includes arts &amp; crafts. Members please contact a mod of your private messaged. 10 - Respect everyone's privacy Being part of this group requires mutual trust. Authentic, expressive discussions make groups great, but may also be sensitive and private. What's shared in the group should stay in the group. We operate a 3 strike system: 1st offense is a 24 hour mute 2nd offense is a 7 day mute 3rd offense is removal from the group However we will remove people earlier if anything is deemed NSFW or if someone is trying to sell account/passwords.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Star Trek
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This Star Trek Group is a safe and friendly place for people to enjoy discussing Star Trek in all its incarnations with keeping with the principle of Infinite Diversity In Infinite Combinations (IDIC) a core belief in the group. 1. Please be respectful of others in the group. Discriminatory behavior based on ethnicity, religion, gender, gender identity, sexual preference or any other perceived difference is not acceptable. 2. Harassment of admins or other group members, whether publicly in the group or privately through messages, is unacceptable and will result in a permanent ban from the group. If you're being harassed, message one of the admins. 3. Spam is going to be deleted and the person will be removed. It's okay to advertise your page here as long as it has to do with Star Trek, but nothing like the "make money with Facebook fast" nonsense. Multiple posts of the same link/article will be removed. 4. Please don't blow up the page with too many posts in a short amount of time. Give others time to post too. 5. Do not re-post or rehash the contents of past threads that have already been deleted. 6. Stay on the topic of the group. The focus of the group is Star Trek. Posts on cross-overs with other series are all right but please concentrate on the Star Trek parts. 7. Given the wide variety of people in the group real life religion and political posts/comments/pics do not belong in here. Those will be removed as soon as an admin sees them. 8. Posts deemed inappropriate will be deleted. If after repeated warnings the individual continues to post inappropriate material, the admins may remove that individual from the group. 9. Don't block any admins. If so, a ban from the group will be the result. 10. Admins must consult with each other before making major changes, including the removal of individuals from this group. 11. Do not post complaints to the group about the admins' management or decisions. If you have a specific grievance, please take this directly to the admins via private message. We deliberately avoid naming and shaming group members so we ask that you do us the same courtesy. 12. You may feel free to debate which series or movie is the best. Just remember to keep post/comments civil and respect your fellow member(s) even if you disagree with them. 13. You may post a photo or link to sell items so long as if it's on eBay, Etsy, Amazon or from your own home as long as they are in a single post. Also, a description must be given of the items 14. Write no negative or hate comments on a celebration post such as a birthday post to an update post on one of the actors or actresses. If so, a warning will be given. If it persists then you'll be removed from the group. 15. NO SPOILERS for new Star Trek episodes are to be posted until 4 days (96 hours) after an episode first airs. 16. No promotion or linking of piracy/streaming sites. Most of all, please enjoy &amp; have fun fellow Trek fans!
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Universal Horror Films
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome all! Celebrating the classic Universal Studios horror films! The period in discussion is generally 1923 (Hunchback of Notre Dame) to 1963 (The Birds), on films made by Universal, but also their silent ancestors (Nosferatu, Caligari) and inspirations, the immediate reincarnations (Hammer) or contemporary cousins from other studios (Mark of the Vampire, White Zombie, Val Lewton's work....). AIP films (such as Corman's Poe series), 1950s Universal Sci-fi, Ed Wood and other B-Movies and pre-1960 horror in general are fair game. GUIDELINES/CONDUCT - Stay on topic. Refrain from modern horror. No Brendan Fraser Mummies or Del Toro Wolfmen please! This is an old-timers group! - No Spamming. When we receive a request for the posting of obvious spam, we typically remove the offending member. Spam includes promotions/contest links. - Be respectful. You may think that The Mummy's Curse is the best of the Lon Chaney Mummy films. But other people may pick Ghost or even Tomb! There are other opinions. Respect them. Discuss, debate, have fun, but be courteous and respectful. - While you are very enthusiastic about your personal projects, this is not a promotion site. If you create art or literature with a direct connection to Universal Monsters, that's one thing. But we do not promote music, websites, indie films, etc. that are simply sci-fi or horror-related but not related to Universal Monsters.

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 OFFICIAL RULES: OVERVIEW - you can post anything that will not offend ANYONE in anyway 1. No posting or commenting hate about other ships and no hate comments towards other members or the admins 2. We support Yaoi and Yuri. SO NO HATE - BUT EXPRESSION RESPECTIVE OPINION IN OPEN DISCUSSION OR DEBATE IS ALLOWED 3. Pictures are to be acceptable for ages fifteen and under, Hentai is not allowed and neither is nudity. 4. We are an Attack On Titan group but you are allowed to post things to do with other anime/manga/cosplay as long as it's something other members will find relatable. And anything else for that matter - I.e personal or general as long as it's within the rules Don’t complain about post diversity 5. Ask permission to advertise anything such as Instagram,groups,pages,Twitter etc 6. If you feel like someone is attacking you in the comment section or through a post, message or tag one of the admins or report to admin DO NOT report directly to Facebook. Please screen shot the conversation as evidence 7. Pretending that art/drawings from Google are yours is illegal and the image will be deleted if it is plagiarised and perpetrator will be banned 8. No political posts 9. "Who should I cosplay as" and "who do you ship me with" posts will be deleted after two hours approx. 10. Porn posts or spam posts of any kind will be removed immediately and you will be banned. No political posts .a little bit of swearing is okay but if you're being horrible you will be banned without warning also. 11. We DO NOT accept self harming posts of any kind (that includes photos of anime characters self harming) if you are feeling depressed please message a friend/family member or call your countries helpline. Also no posts on depression etc 12. No blocking admins from commenting on any post or blocking in general otherwise you will immediately be banned. 13. A SPOILER IS ANYTHING NOT ANIMATED If you have a spoiler please put on your post *SPOILER* and leave MORE THAN 12 spaces down before writing your spoiler. The spoiler MUST be in the “see more” section - if that doesn’t show you need more dots ! Screen shots from manga can be posted in comment section if you want to be considerate. If you want to discuss manga up to date join the “Attack on Titans Manga Fans” group. 14. Please do not insult other people's art without constructive critisism; keep your views and expectations open minded. 15. When commenting on cosplay etc please only give constructive criticism - no hate or trolling - as it will result in a removal warning 16. Keep live videos under 15 (age) Anyone doing anything inappropriate will be barred If you’re are unsure if your post is allowed please message us and wait patiently for a reply.

                 Classic Film Noir Lovers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Classic Film Noir Lovers group! This noir group is devoted to anything related to Classic Film Noirs, the Actors, Actresses, Writers, Producers, Directors, Musical Scores of the noir movies. Classic Film Noir Lovers is for all those that love this genera of film, a type of crime film featuring cynical malevolent characters in a sleazy setting, dark shadows and an ominous atmosphere that is conveyed by shadowy photography and foreboding background music. The Noir Femme Fatale: The promise of adventure, mystery and painful desire, and the promise of mutual commitment, beyond a quick thrill. Enjoy your stay! &lt;3 What is a classic film noir? Click on this site for a short documentary about the Film Noir. http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=K-2y2k_cKr8 THE NOIR FILM LOVERS GROUP MEMBERSHIP RULES Please do not post movies that are not in the classic noir genera. This movie group is strictly for the noir films, all other outside this genera are subject to being removed. Pre-noirs and neo-noir films are welcomed but please limit discussions and post to movies made before 1963 the end of the classic noir period. Non-noir films are subject to be deleted. Respect the opinion of others at all times. Treat others in a discussion as you would want to be treated. Political posts of any kind are not allowed and will be deleted. This is a classic film group, discussions of political events of the day, political opinions, and politics in general are not appropriate for this movie group and should be avoided. Continued abusers will be banned from the group. Also, please do not post any photos, detailed references, videos, or comments with nudity, sex, sexual innuendo, drug use, graphic, gory violence, or obscene language in them. In other words posts not related to classic movies will be removed with or without warning. Anyone that blocks the administrator will be deleted from the group. Obvious SPAM posters will be banned immediately, as well as clear violators of the above mentioned rules. Thank you for your cooperation. Louis B. Caruana, February 23, 2015.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Anime Figures &amp; Plushies - Buy, Sell &amp; Trade
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 🌸RULES 🌸 . You MUST only post items allowed on this page (Anime Figures and/or Plushes) . You MUST state the authenticity of all items . You MUST state the condition of all items . You MUST state the location &amp; currency of the item . You MUST include your own pictures or are able to provide them to buyers . You MUST ask for permission before sharing or linking a new page/group (we need to check for safety and legitimacy) ✅ ITEMS ALLOWED ✅ . Anime figures . Anime plushies . Kawaii/Japanese plushies ⛔️ITEMS NOT ALLOWED INCLUDE ⛔️ . Stationary . Keyrings . Cosplay . Clothes . DVD's . Comic books/manga . Household goods . Unapproved advertising of shops/pages (we need to check these first to make sure they are safe and legitimate) 🌸 ITEM AUTHENTICITY 🌸 When stating item authenticity you must state either 'Authentic/legitimate/licensed' or 'bootleg,fake'. If you are unsure of an item's authenticity, then you must state this too. 🌸 BUYER/SELLER PROTECTION 🌸 We are not responsible for any issues with sellers and sadly we only have the power to ban scammers. To help avoid scammers we recommend: . Using Paypal business helps protect both buyers and sellers. Using it insures you against loss or scamming, allowing you to get your money back from Paypal if something goes wrong . Using tracked or signed postage, again this can help avoid or catch out scammers. . Refusing any purchasing through Paypal friends or through bank transfer, neither of these methods provide buyer protection. ✅Admins you can contact are Jessica Ray and Emily Kate Parsons .✅ 🌸TRADERS!🌸 . YY Kawaii - Instagram https://www.instagram.com/yykawaiimerch . Charmingsushi.co.uk . Middlerealm.co.uk . Amiami.com . Nendoworld.co.uk . Solarisjapan.com . Tofucute.co.uk . Artbox.co.uk .                  Welcome to the official Red Table Talk group! Our community is a place where we can ALL be open to important conversations regarding various topics discussed on and off the Red Table. But like any conversation, here are some things to be mindful of: We all have varying opinions and we welcome you to share those opinions, however this is not the place to dismiss others nor spread hate. The Red Table Talk community is open to everyone, but we prefer to leave hate speech, advertisements and spam off the table. Here's what we'd love for you to do: Be involved in the conversation. Be courteous to everyone's point of view. Be open and share your stories. Be ready every Monday for brand new episodes, only on Facebook Watch! And MOST importantly, be yourself! Remember what this is all about: It’s about three generations of women - Jada Pinkett Smith, her daughter Willow, and mother Adrienne opening their home and inviting all of YOU in to join the conversation. This is the place where we keep that conversation going. Our intergenerational cast has a lot to say and they promise to always: Bring it. Feel it. Share it. Leave it. #AllOnTheTable So we encourage you to do the same 😊 CONTENT USAGE AGREEMENT By commenting in the group, you give Red Table Talk, Facebook and its distributors permission to use your comment, name and profile pic in the show *and* for marketing the show, anytime and anywhere.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 All Day Every Day Anime
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for everyone who loves anime &amp; manga! Pictures, videos, memes, etc are welcome! Open to all fans 😄 This is a group where everyone should have fun! RULES: 1. Any content that doesn't fall under anime, manga or Japanese culture is not allowed such as gaming streams and spam contests/giveaway’s. A contest/giveaway will only be allowed if it comes from an official certified page. Anything else especially if you repeatedly try to share it will get declined or result in a BAN! 2. Post anything vulgar, offensive, inappropriate, or explicitly sexual such as HENTAI, RAPE, furries or beastiality are not allowed! Posting this will result in an immediate BAN! 3. No selfies unless it's cosplay! 4. All posts Must be in English. Posts that aren't in English won't be approved unless they have the Auto-translate button on them. 5. Posting ANYTHING that can be considered racist, sexist, religious or anti-LGBTQ ect. Will Not Be Tolerated!! Bullying, being disrespectful/rude is not allowed. If you disagree with something and you can discuss it in a calm and respectful manner then keep scrolling. Treat this family with respect!! 6. No SPOILERS or Group Chats! If you would like to chat with other members of this group you can join our Discord. 7. Give more than you take! You can share yours or other peoples pages/groups here just no spamming. And we do ask if you are constantly sharing others stuff in return you share our group as well. 8. Selling Is Not Allowed!!! Unless its been posted on an official selling site and it HAS to be anime related. 9. DO NOT PLAGIARIZE IN ANY WAY!!!!! Anyone who tries to pass someone else’s artwork/content etc off as their own will get a warning message from an admin or mod. When posting your own content please include a signature in the photo or a link to your content page for proof of ownership. When posting others content please post a CTTO "credit to the owner" tag at the top of your post. Not following these rules will result in a Ban! **If you have any questions or complaints, please message an Admin and we will do our best to help out. You can comment "Admin" on any post in the group &amp; we'll all get a notification &amp; do our best to resolve it. Don't report anything to FB please &amp; thanks!!
                </div>

                 Expressing love for our waifus, daily posts and general anime shitposting. Biggest waifu group out there. Waifu Hell Discord: https://discord.gg/waifuhell GROUP RULES (Failure to follow these rules will result in a ban) Our rules follow FB Community Standards. -Content that is over-revealing or contains nudity is not allowed. You cannot post "lewds" or "ecchi" in this group. We need to be strict on that to comply with Facebook's own community standards so if its NSFW, don't post it. If you have to question if your post is overly sexual or not then simply don't post it. Failure to comply will result in getting banned from the group. This is to protect the group from being deleted and we have received warnings from Facebook last year. Ever since we implemented this rule and acted strict on it, there have been no issues with Facebook so let us keep it that way. We will comply with Facebook's community standards. -Extreme gore is not allowed (It violates Facebook's standards and so does nudity) -You can't promote/advertise other groups/pages/websites/links. If we let everyone advertise then the group would turn into a bunch of link spam and it would be very unenjoyable. Self promotion is not allowed unless you get approval by an admin. Admins are allowed to share stuff that belong in the the network of groups/pages also administrated by admins of Waifu Hell. A privilege for the admins for putting their time to help with the group. If you want to advertise something of yours please let an admin know first for approval via message. -Spamming is not allowed. Neither is desperate attention seeking. -You cannot post things that are completely off topic from the context of Anime/Manga related content. This includes political posts as well, which are not allowed. Keep your political opinions to yourself and politics out of Waifu Hell. -Rudeness, bashing on other group members for no reason or being racist, targeting a specific member in the group, attacking people, being hostile, making up lies about others etc will not be tolerated. -No excessive whining. This isn't a place for attention seekers who do nothing but promote a negative and boring atmosphere in the group. We reserve the right to remove anyone that is being whiny and annoying. -You can't post major spoilers especially to something recent or not very well known. Don't ruin it for somebody. -Blocking admins is useless because we can still see all of your posts and comments. Anyone blocking an admin thinking they can get away with spamming or other mischief will get banned. -P.assword to join the group: Protein -If someone is banned and would like to be unbanned, they can simply message an admin. We don't gain anything from keeping people banned and will be happy to un-ban anyone provided that they will follow the group's rules. -If you don't like/agree/follow with the group rules you can leave. Nobody is forcing you to stay For further questions please contact an admin.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Podcasters' Support Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Podcasters' Support Group! READ THIS BEFORE PROCEEDING. This group is a meeting place for podcasters old and new to chat, swap tips, seek advice about technical stuff or audio creativity or general podcast-related business; and, overall, it's here for us to support each other through the lonely grind that podcasting sometimes/often/always is. We sometimes get together in real life, too, so look out for details of upcoming meetups, and share yours if you've set one up. Do not use this group to swap reviews, to sell services that are unrelated to podcasts, or to relentlessly promote your show/yourself. The time and place to publicise your work is the Weekend Wankfest, which runs from Friday-Sunday, so comment with a link to your show on those threads. Individual promotional posts will be binned. Before you post a post, run through the following checklist: Is the post podcast-related? YES Is it flagrant self-promotion? NO Does it read like spam? NO Is it an inspirational slogan against a background of eg a serene lake? OH HELL NO Is it asking people to swap reviews? NO Is it selling a service that is unrelated to podcasting? NO Is it a screenshot of your download numbers? NO (Unless you have spotted something odd about them and wanted a second opinion.) Is it a link to your YouTube video/Facebook Live? NO, COS IS NOT THE RIGHT GROUP FOR THAT Is it some clickbait bullshit? YOU'LL NEVER BELIEVE WHAT HAPPE- no, it is not. Is it a photo of your mic next to your laptop? NO, WE ALL KNOW WHAT A MIC NEXT TO A LAPTOP LOOKS LIKE Is it a photo of your new mic/headphones/mixer still in its box? NO. IT IS NOT A PHOTO OF A BOX. Also! This group has been running for years, so your question may have answered before. Search the group for keywords if you want to know about, for example: Hosting options Equipment options Distribution platforms Recording in separate locations Marketing, and growing your audience Rules about using copyrighted music in a podcast? Private message etiquette: ONLY send a PM to another group member if they have given you permission to do so. If you spam PSG members' PMs, you'll be blocked from the group. Please don't PM me asking me whether it's OK for you to post a post - while I appreciate your care, my attentions are already oversubscribed trying to administrate the posts that ARE posted in the group. If yours obeys the rules above, post it. If you're not sure, do go ahead and post it, and an admin will deal with it if necessary. DO feel free to PM me if another group member is mistreating you or others, though. This may seem like a lot, but I'm in other podgroups that are cesspits full of jerkwater, and I want this one to stay friendly, helpful, civilised and upbeat, with minimal passive-aggression, aggressive-aggression, micsplaining, shitposting and boregasms. But I trust you. You're a smart person. You read this far; you get it. Thanks for joining - glad to have you here! Helen Zaltzman
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Casting Directors for Actors
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group for anybody in the arts. The current membership consists mostly of actors and casting directors, associates and assistants. There are a fair number of agents and managers, directors and producers and crew members of all kinds. I created this group around 2007 as a means for actors to ask questions and seek advice directly from casting professionals. We had about 300 members back then. Currently, we have just about 50,000 world wide members and the group has grown into a place to discuss anything industry related, seek or give advice, resume, and reel and even post and casting calls. If you want your headshots to be critiqued, please post them at https://www.facebook.com/groups/headshotcritique A team of 4 volunteer countless hours to keep this group running. Me - Jeremy Gordon http://www.imdb.com/name/nm1873883 I cast feature films, TV shows, webseries, commercials, short films, etc. I have been casting for 13 years and have worked on everything from We’re The Millers, Think Like A Man, We Bought A Zoo, The Wolverine, Hawaii 5-0 and Hell On Wheels. I spent 2 years on the Board of Directors of the Casting Society of America and am a member of the Academy of Television Arts and Sciences. I love food, especially cheese. I’m constantly on the go unless I’m tinkering in my garden. And I still think The West Wing is one of the best TV shows of all time! Edward Hong is an actor in LA. http://www.imdb.me/edwardhong who is known as the Cinnabon Monster (www.cinnabonmonster.com), and through that, has gotten CD's, industry folks, and the Cinnabon company itself as well as the CEO to know him by name. He is also a great source of food recommendations (but only when they're fatty). Ben Whitehair is an actor in LA. http://www.imdb.com/name/nm3290049 Ben knows a LOT of things about a LOT of things, both entertainment industry related, politics, business, etc. Really and truly. He’s my go to guy for just about anything. He has mastered the art of social media for actors and is the man behind Actor Tweetup: https://www.facebook.com/groups/LAActorsTweetup/ Annie Wood is an actress and writer in LA. http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0747788 Annie is one the nicest human beings I have ever met. She’s also one of the funniest peeps ever. She has a lot of info she’s happy to share. Simply put, she writes some of the funniest and most heartfelt stuff out there. From scenes to pilots to features and webseries, I love everything she writes (and I’ve even cast some of it, too, such as - https://www.facebook.com/pages/Karmas-a-Bitch-the-series/1536598733248203?fref=ts There are rules we require all members to follow and we do enforce them. There isn't enough space to list them here so please take a moment to look at the FILE called "Casting Directors For Actors - GROUP RULES" or search the wall for the same file. Please and thank you.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Film Noir
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 What is "film noir"? It's a universe of fallen angels and black angels... raw deals and pitfalls... roadblocks and detours... and cities that never sleep. Film noir is a shadowy world of existential loners, of chumps who willingly accept their downfall, of mobsters looking for a taste of the high life, of women both redemptive and destructive, of desperate men who just want an even break. Noir is a dark city of blind alleys, losers' lanes, and side streets leading to dead ends. And even in the outskirts of the city, somewhere in the night, a devil is thumbing a ride. Noir is inhabited by hard-boiled private detectives, double-dealing dames, carnival hustlers, psychotic killers, disillusioned artists, broken-down boxers, and a million others from every dark corner of society. The noir universe is a place where (in the words of Roberts in DETOUR): "Fate, or some mysterious force, can put the finger on you or me for no good reason at all." Film noir or "black film" is a French term describing the dark side of American movies throughout the 1940s and 1950s. Noir was the perfect hybrid of German Expressionist cinematography and the hard-boiled tradition of pulp fiction. Noir inhabited a certain time frame in American cinema and reflected the growing cynicism prevalent in a post-war America. The classic period is generally considered to have begun in 1941 with THE MALTESE FALCON and lasting until 1958's TOUCH OF EVIL. Many of these creative films were more ambiguous extensions of the 1930s gangster dramas, but noir is not a genre. It's a visual style that incorporates more than just crime films. The style, made up of such elements as low-key lighting, night settings, and compositional tension, can be found in many genres, from horror films to Westerns. Filmmakers did not set out to make film noir and were not aware of the term or of the conventions modern audiences now associate with it. What moviemakers depicted onscreen at the time was merely their subconscious response to the reality of world affairs. Some of the themes the films addressed included disillusionment, paranoia, alienation, and sexual obsession. The themes had their hard-boiled roots in the works of authors such as Dashiell Hammett, Raymond Chandler, James M. Cain, and Cornell Woolrich. Many of the onscreen crime dramas were the progeny of these American writers. However, there was a distinctly European influence as well on how these stories were translated to the screen. The stylistics owe much to the German Expressionist movement, and many of the filmmakers had come from Germany and eastern Europe: directors like Fritz Lang, Billy Wilder, Otto Preminger, Robert Siodmak, and Edgar G. Ulmer. Included in this group of craftsmen are cinematographers such as John Alton, whose visions of light helped define the visual grammar of film noir. Economics, if not the artistic intentions of the filmmakers, also had a lot to do with how the films were made. Some of the best were "B" movies shot cheaply at smaller studios like RKO. Often, the style transcended their story-- how the stories were told could be far more interesting than what they told. The movies of this period in the 1940s and '50s reflected a shadowy world where the stylistics of Expressionist lighting could meet the realism of on-location shooting. The legacy of film noir pervades popular culture today with conscious attempts by modern filmmakers to mimic the past under the label of neo-noir. But the images from the classic period are ingrained in our cinematic consciousness. Who can forget Richard Widmark in KISS OF DEATH pushing a helpless mother in her wheelchair down a flight of stairs, or Rita Hayworth's striptease to the tune of "Put the Blame on Mame" in GILDA, or James Cagney's Cody Jarrett making it to the top of the world in a blaze of WHITE HEAT. When we think of noir, what comes to mind but a tough detective in a trench coat and fedora-- and the mysterious femme fatale out to ruin him. We think of the stories told in voiceover and through flashback... stories about double crosses-- and criss crosses. In this group--"Film Noir Style: Through a Lens Darkly"-- we will take a serious look at film noir, penetrating deep into the elements that make up the style. We will also examine the cinematographers behind these classic films; this is the page for those who appreciate cameramen like John Alton, Nicholas Musaraca, Joseph LaShelle, Lee Garmes, Milton Krasner, and Franz Planer. And most importantly, we will honor directors like Anthony Mann, Robert Siodmak, Fritz Lang, Jacques Tourneur, Robert Wise, Edgar G. Ulmer, Nicholas Ray, Andre de Toth, Raoul Walsh, and so many others. Let Robert Mitchum, Ida Lupino, Robert Ryan, Gene Tierney, Richard Widmark, Lizabeth Scott, Dick Powell, Gloria Grahame, and Dan Duryea be your guides through cinema's seamy underworld.
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Studio Ghibli - WORLDWIDE FANGROUP
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Studio Ghibli (スタジオジブリ ) es un estudio japonés de animación, considerado por la crítica especializada y muchos cinéfilos como uno de los mejores estudios de animación del mundo en la actualidad. Fundado en 1985, está dirigido por el galardonado director Hayao Miyazaki (宮崎 駿 Miyazaki Hayao) junto a su amigo y mentor Isao Takahata. Sus orígenes datan de 1983, con la película Nausicäa del Valle del Viento (風の谷のナウシカ Kaze no tani no Naushika, 1984). _________________________________________________________ Studio Ghibli is a japanese animation film studio best known for its anime feature films. Eight of Studio Ghibli's films are among the 15 highest-grossing anime films made in Japan, many of their works have won the Animage Anime Grand Prix award, and four have won the Japan Academy Prize for Animation of the Year. HERE you will find a list of the movies made by the studio: -http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Studio_Ghibli -http://www.onlineghibli.com/films.php

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to ONE PIECE FAN GROUP! *°*RULES*°* 1. Respect Everyone. Racism, Discrimination, Homophobia and Bullying will not be tolerated. Breaking this Rule will lead to being kicked and banned from the Group. 2. No Pornographic Content. This includes hentai, pornographic videos and nude images. Breaking this rule will lead to being kicked and banned from the group. 3 Speak English One Piece Fan Group is an International Group. Meaning, that all members reside from different parts of the World so English will be the neutral Language. Breaking this rule will be met with warnings from Admins and moderators. Refusing to adhere to the rule and ignoring the Warnings will lead to being kicked and banned from the Group. 4. No Blocking any Admins or Moderators! 5. One Piece Related Content ONLY! Posting other shows and other content that have no relation to One Piece whatsoever will be deleted. (For example; selfies, pictures, Youtube/Facebook videos, website links etc.) Repetitively breaking this rule and ignoring the warnings from Admins and Moderators will result in being kicked and banned from the group. 6. If someone tries to start a Conflict with you then notify Us! We'll deal with it immediately. 7. NO ADVERTISEMENT! Members posting Advertisements such as; Asking to like a Page, advertising Businesses, selling Products or Services will all be kicked and banned. 8. Spoilers are allowed but be sure to put Spoiler Alert on your posts. Ignoring warnings from Moderators or Admins will get your post deleted and repetitively committing the rule break will get you kicked out. 9. No Spamming! Repetitively posting the same content in one day will get your post deleted. This goes with the comment section as well, if a member keeps commenting the same comment over and over again will result in being kicked out. 10. No Illegal Video Uploads or Links of full Episodes and Movies of One Piece. These videos will be deleted, continually posting these videos will get you kicked and banned. We are all One piece Fans here and want to watch all the One Piece episodes. But we also respect the copyrights ownership of One Piece as animators and manga artist like Oda, who work hard day in and day out to produce great content. As True One Piece Fans, we promote the legal way of viewing the Anime, any full free and illegal episodes or movies of Onepiece posted on the group will be deleted. PS: If there is something wrong going in the group or if you find someone breaking these rules or if you find any vulgar post or comment then Please assist us by /Reporting/ to Us. We'll handle the Rest. Admins ♕Ace Redfield ♕Dante Jäger Moderators ♗Ros Delos Reyes ♗Akshay Ashara ♗Trafalgar D. Bojana ♗Zachary D Corr ♗Selfa Delos Reyes ♗Raquel Bailon-Baltazar ♗Krishna Mohan Visit our One Piece Page too: fb.com/OPBest.FanPage Keep Calm &amp; Love One Piece! :)

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is the JOHN WAYNE fan club – one of the finest groups you’re ever likely to find on Facebook. We talk, share stories, information, the occasional link to movies &amp; music, &amp; we have some of the very best images you’ll ever see. We pride ourselves on our neighborly membership. Here at JWfc, Duke is very much alive. We welcome those who share a mutual respect for Duke, &amp; all he stands for. "Copyright Disclaimer Under Section 107 of the Copyright Act 1976, allowance is made for "fair use" for purposes such as criticism, comment, news reporting, teaching, scholarship, &amp; research. Fair use is a use permitted by copyright statute that might otherwise be infringing. Non-profit, educational or personal use tips the balance in favour of fair use. We, who post images (moving or otherwise) on the JWfc do not own the rights. Such images are used to promote comment &amp; critique in a non-profit manner for educational fair use. Due to possible infringement of copyright laws any artistic images that are created should be posted on this site for entertainment purposes only. TRADING: Members are asked not to "solicit for sale" any images or items on the JWfc Forum. We ask those wishing to trade to redirect individuals to the private chat/messaging facility &amp;/or their own Facebook account or website. Those who post links to other web-pages that are clearly promoting the sale of any goods will have their post deleted &amp; may be removed. Those who target/approach JWfc members by private message in an attempt to sell goods will be immediately removed and blocked (our members are loyal and keep us informed). PROMOTIONAL: Those hoping to promote their business, website, Facebook page or product (book, movie, etc.) should initially contact the Sheriff, Chas Birch. Those who do not will be removed from JWfc. Full RULES are located in the 'About' section.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Podcasts!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group for sharing, discovering, and discussing podcasts. Feel free to add anyone who might enjoy discovering new podcasts or anyone who has a podcast to share. Group Rules from the Admins: 1. Promotional Posts This group DOES allow self-promotion of your own podcast. However, do not abuse this privilege and spam the group. The mods do have the discretion to remove spammers. 2. Cross Promotion Cross promotion is encouraged. Reaching out should be specific about guest requests or specific episodes or topics. Like for like, follow for follow, etc. is not allowed. See Rule 3. 3. No Review Swapping, etc. We do not allow review swapping, like swapping, follow swapping, etc. Offending posts will be removed and the poster may also be removed at the mod's discretion. 4. All Posts Should Be About Podcasting There is a very blurry line between video blogging, streaming, and video podcasting; thus, it will be up to the mods discretion whether a post is podcasting related. 5. Be Kind and Courteous We're all in this together to create a welcoming environment. Let's treat everyone with respect. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. 6. No Hate Speech or Bullying Make sure everyone feels safe. Bullying of any kind isn't allowed, and degrading comments about things like race, religion, culture, sexual orientation, gender or identity will not be tolerated. 7. Respect Everyone's Privacy Being part of this group requires mutual trust. Authentic, expressive discussions make groups great, but may also be sensitive and private. What's shared in the group should stay in the group.
