                 Welcome to one of the newest and fastest growing Anime and Nerd groups on Facebook. Please read full description to understand how this group is run. Otherwise you will be confused and complain about something not being approved.. don't say you weren't warned.. IF YOU DONT READ, YOU LOSE YOUR RIGHT TO COMPLAIN WITH VALIDATION. {Now With a Monthly Activity of 4.5 million!} + posts, +comments,+ reactions. ⚖️ MAIN GROUP RULES⚔️ **THERE ARE AROUND 100 ADDITIONAL GUIDELINES IN OUR ANNOUNCEMENTS SECTION. BE SURE TO CLICK "SEE ALL" TO VIEW THEM.** [Rules are subject to change at any time] 1) Allowed topics are anything related to Anime, Manga, Cosplay, Videogames, Science and Popular Culture. Repeat posts will be approved in a random limited interval. 2) This is the internet and shit gets crazy. Try to behave yourself and keep things under the radar of the mighty Zuck. We don't want endless shitposting either. 3) Everything that happens in this group must also adhere to the Facebook Guidelines. No nudity, Racism, homophobia, gaybashing, etc. 4) Don't advertise your shit here without asking. Groups, group chats, youtubes, GoFundMe etc. if you would like to negotiate a deal on advertising, message the page. 5) For now any deathbattles/ vs battles will be very limited. Admins and mods will review each one and see if it fits the quality standards. No spite posts or repetitive posts we've already seen. 6) DO NOT REPORT POSTS TO FACEBOOK Report to ADMIN any posts that violate rules. &lt;- Please utilize this feature to help us deal with certain posts as fast as possible. Only report posts that break rules. DO NOT report posts that follow rules. Doing this will get you removed from the group as a warning. 7) Our moderators are trained extensively to be the most unbiased mediators of the group. So it's very important to listen to them, for they know the best interests of the group. 8) If you have any problems let us know. If you think a mod is in the wrong or abusing power, contact our linked page for support. We run a fair but strict group, all admin decisions are final. 9) Do not message admins. Just post or comment and ask for a random mod in the group, at least one will usually be active. Or message our page for more serious inquiries. 10) Lastly If anything else isn't listed here in the first ten rules please refer to our announcement posts section to see what else is allowed in the group. GROUP POSTS SCHEDULE. Any day with a ⭐ next to it will not have mainstream posts approved that day. Including but not limited to Naruto, DB, One Piece, h×h, black clover, my hero, attack on titan, and demon slayer. Subject to change. Sunday⭐ Monday Tuesday ⭐ Wednesday Thursday ⭐ Friday Saturday 💎 both allowed. Non mainstream will be prioritized. Full details on all our rules and guidelines can be found here. ⬇️⬇️⬇️ https://www.facebook.com/groups/1367928843374571/permalink/1615528918614561/

THE WALL WILL BE SHUT OFF DURING PREMIERE DAYS FOR 24 HOURS TO ALLOW FOR ALL TIME ZONES TO VIEW. There is a group hosted Event for discussing new episodes live, before the spoiler ban is lifted. Want to connect with other fans in your area?                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Universal Horror &amp; Classic Creatures
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 We love the classic monsters and classic horror, science fiction and fantasy films. Anything from German Expressionist Silent Classics, Universal Studios and others of the 1930s and 1940s, Hammer and Amicus films of the 1950s through the 1970s. We are indeed speaking of film monsters, not real life ones. No "real life" horrors. No serial killers. No slasher films. No politics of any kind. No nudity or anything that will get the group in trouble with FB rules. No cheesecake, photoshopped or otherwise. There are plenty of other FB groups for that sort of thing. Photos should be film related. Please do not just post "title cards". PLEASE do not "spam" the group with multiple posts; either put them in one post with multiple pictures, or save them so as to give others a chance. Please make sure that the images have decent resolution. As a group, we should keep it interesting and high quality and if the images are too "lo-rez", it just looks haphazard. No watch parties. Even a lot of things that were formerly considered public domain are currently being restored and under license. This also includes links to films in their entirety. Segments/portions of films only are OK. We do not want to be shut down because of this. It isn't worth it. Thank you and Enjoy!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The New York Times Podcast Club
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The NYT Podcast Club is a community of podcast lovers who discuss one episode of one podcast every week — basically, a book club for podcasts. It's a forum for conversation, analysis and spreading the love of podcasts. (It's also an online extension of a club started among NYT employees.) Every Monday, we’ll post this week's episode for discussion, and we'll keep it up throughout the week with daily discussion posts. A few rules: 1. Keep your criticism constructive and your disagreements respectful. We encourage lively debate and discussion! But be nice. 2. We've designated Self-Promotion Saturdays as a chance for your to share your work underneath our Saturday post. But otherwise, this isn't the place for that. (And no PR pitches meant for NYT reporters, please. They'll be deleted immediately.) 3. No personal attacks. Comments that stray from a tone that fosters productive dialogue will be removed. Rude behavior and insults (including calling someone who disagrees with you a "troll") won't be tolerated. 4. We're here to discuss podcasts. Off-topic posts and comments won't be allowed here. 5. If there's an episode or show you want to share with the group, please wait until we ask for your recommendations on Suggestion Sunday. This is a crowd-sourced idea to keep the group's timeline more focused on discussions. Just joining us? Want to see how we chatted about a past episode? This album is a round-up of all past episode discussions. Jump in if you've still got something to add: http://nyti.ms/2vqd6xS To learn about our privacy practices, please read our Privacy Policy at: https://nytimes.com/privacy.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Frugal Filmmaker
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 We look at ways to stretch your microscopic movie budget without sacrificing quality. Frugal Filmmaker Guidelines and Rules of Conduct ￼ 01. Absolutely NO FLAMING, NAME CALLING OR PERSONAL ATTACKS. Mutual respect and civilized conversation is the required norm. 02. This is a FILMMAKING site, no general computer- or photography support-group. Please keep it on topic! 03. No THREAD HIJACKING. Start another thread if you have a different topic. 04. Please keep the cursing/profanity to a minimum. Excessive amounts will be removed without warning. 05. Be RESPECTFUL to others. Form normal sentences, don't go all-caps. Respect their choice of religion, operating systems (we hate Mac vs PC debates) and way of living. 06. No PORNOGRAPHIC or GORE posts. Keep also in mind the standards of other cultures than yours. 07. Do not post PERSONAL/PRIVATE INFORMATION (i.e. addresses, phone numbers, passwords, personal identification numbers, images) or any other information considered private without the express permission of the individual/company. 08. Observe all COPYRIGHT LAWS. 09. You will not discuss, suggest, engage, or encourage any ILLEGAL ACTIVITIES. Especially regarding software pirating - that includes "Jokes" about it, this is serious! 10. No senseless ADVERTISING in the group - if you want to post adverts, please message one of the admins. 11. This group is not a place for PAGE/SITE PIMPING. Post if you need feedback, but please respect this is no info-dump! 12. Advertising or site pimping should be done with respect to the group. There will be exceptions to rules on case by case basis. If you have any questions, please reach out to one of the admins. 13. No SPAMMING. In general as well as multiple post to same topic, use the search and bump those threads instead; Spam will be removed without warning. Please use Facebooks REPORT-Function instead of tagging admins or commenting on Spam! 14. We try to not be too harsh, but for violations we have a 3-strike-system. In special cases we reserve the right to ban instantly at admin discretion. 15. You are free to sell and buy things on the Selling-Page on a private basis, however note that transactions are not administrated and are on your own risk. If you want to sell things commercially, please message one of the admins.
                </div>

                 ChooseFI
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ChooseFI.com is a group that serves the audience of the ChooseFI Radio Podcast as well as the greater FI community. The podcast airs every Monday and Friday. Monday introduces a new topic or idea and Friday brings in the community's feedback and ideas. We are not dogmatic here about any single approach to Financial Independence but want to foster conversation that allows all of us to reach our goal of financial independence faster. The path this community chooses to follow to reach FI will be incredibly diverse but the conversation is guaranteed to be fascinating. Our only dogma is that you Take Action. Want to support what we do? Here are a few easy win-win ways that would better your life while costing you no money: 1. Sign up for a high-yield savings account with CIT Bank: choosefi.com/CIT 2. Crushed debt and ready to start saving for the future while hacking your taxes? Open a tax-advantaged account with Mi Finance at choosefi.com/m1. 3. Track your net worth with Personal Capital: choosefi.com/pc 4. Want to travel the country and the world for almost free? Check out our free travel rewards course at choosefi.com/travel.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Hayao Miyazaki Fan Club
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group for people who like or love Hayao Miyazaki, and maybe even a few other studio ghibli related directors too. This group is for fun you are allowed to discuss whatever you want here as long as it's related to studio Ghibli and Miyazaki. RULES OF ENGAGEMENT Hello and welcome to the Hayao Miyazaki Fan Club! We're growing every day, and as such I'd like to go over the rules for everyone. 1) Unrelated SPAM posts will NOT BE TOLERATED. This includes profanity and posts of a sexually explicit nature. This is a family group, and we admins intend to keep it that way. These posts will be removed, and the user banned. Consider this your warning, as you'll get none otherwise. 2) While we understand that not everyone has the means to build their own home library of Studio Ghibli movies, we do not promote illegal streaming sites here. You won't be immediately banned, but you shall be warned about it with the post promptly removed. UPDATE: Currently North American patrons can purchase and download digital Studio Ghibli films on a variety of Streaming channels: AppleTV, Amazon, Google Play, Playstation Store, Microsoft, and Fandango NOW. You may reach all channel's Ghibli selections here: https://www.gkidsdigital.com/?utm_source=gkids&amp;utm_medium=site&amp;utm_campaign=socialdec17 Non-North American patrons will be able to stream Studio Ghibli films on Netflix beginning in February 2020. Here is the schedule of movie releases on Netflix: https://i-d.vice.com/en_uk/article/epgxep/studio-ghibli-film-release-netflix-in-2020 3) Please keep in mind that this club is NOT a general club about Anime, but exclusively Hayao Miyazaki and Studio Ghibli in general. Unrelated posts, even if they are not considered SPAM (see rule #1) will be removed at the moderators' discretion. There must be hundreds, if not thousands of more general Anime clubs on Facebook. This is a closed club about Studio Ghibli. 4)Be considerate on potential spoilers. Not all of our members have seen every Studio Ghibli movie. Posts that reveal important/turning point scenes to Studio Ghibli movies are subject to removal. 5) Please visit the Ghibli character pages by fellow admin, Paolo Sardi at https://www.facebook.com/Studio-Ghibli-1529321324054656/. They're in the "Like" Section of the group! 6) My Personal Kiki Fanfic: Kiki's Special Delivery! Short read to follow up the movie. https://www.fanfiction.net/s/12068844/1/Kiki-s-Special-Delivery Have fun and Enjoy!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Silent Film Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the largest Facebook Group dedicated to silent movies! In an attempt to promote silent cinema, this group is trying to compile a list of silent cinema resources so that silent film fans, wherever they are, can connect with local organizations and events. If you are aware of an organization that is doing something related to silent cinema, please contact the administrator with its name, location, website, and email address. Please remember to sign the petition to get Edna Purviance, Charlie Chaplin's leading lady, a star on the Hollywood Walk of Fame. It can be found at: http://www.petitiononline.com/EdnaStar/petition.html This group is a fan group for silent cinema lovers. Though we do not necessarily hate talking pictures, we love the genius of silent films. We love silent movies like City Lights, Seven Chances, Andalusian Dog, The Cabinet of Dr. Caligari, Warning Shadows, Safety Last, Battleship Potemkin, He Who Gets Slapped, The Passion of Joan of Arc, Pandora's Box, Phantom of the Opera, Laugh Clown Laugh, Nosferatu, The Mystery of Leaping Fish, The Gold Rush, Ten Days That Shook The World, Treasures From a Chest, The It Girl, Modern Times, Napolean, The Sheik, Queen Kelly, Steamboat Bill Jr., The Kid, The Eagle, Our Hospitality, The Son of Sheik, Foolish Wives, The Hypocrites, Within Our Gates, Broken Blossoms, Metropolis, Faust, and many others. Finally, a place for people to appreciate Charlie Chaplin, Buster Keaton, Harold Lloyd, Mary Pickford, Gloria Swanson, Clara Bow, Theda Bara, Rudolph Valentino, Zasu Pitts, Erich Von Stroheim, Fritz Lang, Lon Chaney Sr., Douglas Fairbanks Sr., Louise Brooks, Stan Laurel, Abel Gance, Keystone Kops, Carl Dreyer, Edna Purviance, Sergei Eisenstein, Oscar Micheaux, Charley Chase, Lois Weber, and other geniuses of the silent era. What is your favorite silent film? Is there a silent movie you like that you want to tell us about? 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Cosplay Sales 2.0
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Heya! We're all so happy you want to be part of our community, you're all welcome! Just please respect the rules; 1. Understand as you post something, it must be approved by one admin. 2. Realize there are some children in this group. Keep your comments age-appropriate. ---Doesn't mean cosplays like Kill la Kill aren't allowed! 3. Block an Admin and you will be Permanently removed. 4. All posts must follow the guidelines; •Must be in English. Have trouble translating? Contact us! •All payments must be made through Goods and Services by PayPal. •Commissioners must have a public portfolio available as well as feedback. •Only three bumps allowed per week on your post. Special circumstances if it's an urgent sale; contact admins regarding it. •Admins are allowed to add rules as needed. ☆General Selling Post Information☆ Must have: 1. Location 2. Price stated, and if it's a negotiable price. 3. Measurements (if applicable) 4. Shipping. 5. Worn? Brand New? 6. Handmade. 7. Any flaws. 8. ISO/WTB/WTT/WTS COMMISSIONER POSTING INFORMATION •Commissioners must contact one of the admins in order to have their post approved. Just posting won't work. •Portfolio posts are allowed, one bump per week! •If you feel like someone is low balling you, contact us! We'll help you as much as we can. **COMMISSIONING? HERE'S WHAT YOU NEED TO KNOW!** •Understand that the commissioners have to make a profit from this. •Provide many, many, many, photo references. Not every commissioner is going to know that anime, but they still might be the best for the job! •Make sure your budget is reasonable. Ex; You can't ask for a wig like Goku for 10 dollars. The wig base alone can be $60 not including the blood, sweat, and tears of the commissioner •State when you need the piece by! Once again, reasonability! ☆Commission rules☆ 1. Posts looking to commission something must include a budget, deadline, location, and picture(s). 2. Please understand that a low budget for most things won't be able to work with commissions. You might want to try having a flexible budget if you're not sure how the pricing is. 3. Please have both a reasonable budget and a reasonable deadline. Most commissioners won't be able to do last minute projects. 4. Commissioners must be approved by an admin. Contact any of us to get approved. 5. Approved commissioners will be listed in an album so everyone knows who's safe to work with 6. Commissioners must have a public portfolio available and feedback 7. Commissioners can make a portfolio post that includes max 5 photos of your work, a link to your page, and can be bumped once every week. 8. If you're a commissioner commenting on a post, you must link your page
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 MSnbc = Maddow Station = Rachel Lawrence Joy
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 MS=Maddow Station, The Place for Politics, with Lawrence, Joy, Chris, Steve, Ari... We are Mad about Maddow, Rachel fanatics. The purpose of this group is to discuss Rachel Maddow, the venue which sponsors her platform (MSnbc), and the topics discussed there. All people who participate here should be treated with respect and striving for the high journalistic standards of Rachel Maddow. This unofficial fan group has no affiliation with Rachel Maddow, MSNBC or NBC. Please avoid using the "share" button on other page postings. There's a way to cut and paste text, or post a picture directly, without using the "share" button. See instructions here: https://m.facebook.com/groups/934180059972925?view=permalink&amp;id=970462816344649 Please limit indirect posting of memes or shared text. Please directly text a description explaining the purpose of what you might post by way of graphic. Let us have mutual respect for everyone here. No Rachel slurs are permitted in this group. Personal confrontations and replies to posts not related to the scope and spirit of the thread, post, or this group may be deleted. Continued inappropriate replies or posts may result in deletion of the offender. This may be based on feedback from you in private messages. There is no discrimination in this group regarding political views, religion, race, culture, sexual, intellectual orientation, where a person was born, or age. It is the interest of our Administration to keep this a growing family. Feel free to make friends and have personal discussions with them on your own timeline, IM, or personal messages. CONDUCT ("You're Fired") Only respectful, intelligent, civil discourse, using standard English is permitted to participate in this group. This is not censorship. It is the way Rachel Maddow conducts herself as well. Please tag me in a reply or post of any member who is not behaving properly in this group. All you need to do is type "@" symbol, and then immediately start typing my name, Shelly Betancourt. Rachel Maddow does not shout or use profanity. She treats people with respect with intelligent, thought provoking responses. If you do not behave in a similar manner, then you'll be "fired." When you are told that you are fired, you are deleted from the group and possibly even blocked so that you cannot even see the group. This is not censorship. This is called behaving like a mature adult and not like a trump. If you have been deleted, you can reapply. But you must also pm me to discuss why you're appealing the decision. A 2nd offense after being readmitted into the group, will result in your being permanently blocked from the group. If you're blocked, you won't be able to even read group posts, and may not appeal the decision. Shelly Betancourt, 9/15/17 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Old Time Radio Researchers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  The OTRR Group is a community of enthusiastic fans, avid listeners, and strong supporters of “Old Time Radio". The group’s goals include restoring, preserving and sharing the classic shows from what is commonly known as the "Golden Age of Radio" (1930-1960). The OTRR Group, comprised of a diverse world wide group of volunteers, has undertaken many ongoing projects and continues to work hard to preserve our wonderful radio heritage. Please check out our Main Home Page- http://www.otrr.org/index.htm . Also please visit our library at: http://www.otrrlibrary.org/index.html The group is open to all people of all colors and religions who ask for membership. Please post only items about old time radio, and other nostalgic items. No racial material, ethnic slurs or religious jokes will be tolerated. If you post such material, it will be deleted by our administrators and you will be banned and prevented from ever joining the group again.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Pre-Code Hollywood (1929-34): Sin on Celluloid
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Join us as we celebrate pre-Codes, the “raw stuff of American culture, unvarnished and unveiled.” Please LABEL your posts. unlabeled posts will be deleted. NO nude photos allowed. They will be deleted too. Thanks! FOR THE PURPOSES OF THIS GROUP the term "Pre-code" refers to an ERA, i.e. films made IN Hollywood (or the USA in general) between January 1, 1929, and June 30, 1934, silent or sound. That doesn't mean that's what we think the definition of "pre-code" is. It's simply the most objective way to set a solid guideline for posting. The PRE-CODE ERA was a period of filmmaking (1929-34) that featured a more laidback atmosphere. “More unbridled, salacious, subversive, and just plain bizarre than what came afterwards, they look like Hollywood cinema but the moral terrain is so off-kilter they seem imported from a parallel universe,” remarked historian Thomas Doherty. Will H. Hays had been recruited by the Hollywood studios in 1922 to help restore Hollywood’s tainted image brought on by a series of scandals. In 1929, Catholic Martin Quigley, editor of the trade MOTION PICTURE HERALD, and Jesuit priest Father Daniel A. Lord created a code of standards and submitted it to the studios. While the Production Code was adopted in 1930, it was not strictly enforced; therefore, films during this time would often include sexual innuendo, illegal drugs, scantily-clad women, rape, infidelity, abortion, children born out of wedlock, violence and homosexuality, among other later taboo subjects; it was a world where crime *did* pay. At the end of ’33 and the beginning of 1934, the Catholic Legion of Decency fought with a renewed vigor against what they considered the immorality of films. This, combined with the threat of a government takeover of film censorship, brought about a new Motion Picture Production Code, with rules of what was now forbidden on screen; a rigidly enforced crackdown took place as the studios sought the Production Code’s seal of approval before a film could be released. July 1, 1934, signaled the end of the pre-Code era. Wrote historian Thomas Doherty in PRE-CODE HOLLYWOOD SEX, IMMORALITY AND INSURRECTION IN AMERICAN CINEMA, 1930-1934: “American cinema changed. During that month, the Production Code Administration, popularly known as the Hays Office, began to regulate, systematically and scrupulously, the content of Hollywood motion pictures. For the next thirty years, cinematic space was a patrolled landscape with secure perimeters and well-defined borders. Adopted under duress at the urging of priests and politicians, Hollywood's in-house policy of self-censorship set the boundaries for what could be seen, heard, even implied on screen. Not until the mid-1950s did cracks appear in the structure and not until 1968, when the motion picture industry adopted its alphabet ratings system, did the Code edifice finally come crumbling down.” 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Star Wars fans who actually like the movies
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  This group is meant to be a place for all Star Wars related discussion and fun. All Star Wars movies, expanded universe, art, memes, books, games, cartoons, comics are allowed as long as it doesn’t break the group’s or Facebook rules. The requirement is simply to like ALL 11 movies. The Prequels, The Originals, The Sequels, Rogue One and Solo Star Wars has something for everyone to love. Even if you dislike some aspect, you will be expected to debate respectfully and constructively with members. We may hail from different regions but we all are coming here to become immersed in a galaxy far, far away The purpose of this group is to be a fun safe place to discuss our mutual love of all things Star Wars. May the Force Be With You Always

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Beautiful/Anonymous: The Community
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Beautiful/Anonymous is a podcast on the Earwolf network. Each episode, one random phone caller gets on the line with host Chris Gethard. The caller is allowed to say whatever they want as long as they remain anonymous. Chris is not allowed to hang up. Those are the only two rules. If you have a call you'd like to make to the show but don't want to risk being stuck on hold, you can call the voicemail line at 802-39-BEAUT (802-392-3288) or submit a quick story to the Stuck on Hold text series (every Friday). There are really only a few rules here 1) Don't be a troll/jerk and no name calling. You are allowed to disagree, you are allowed to say you don't like episodes, you are allowed to be in a bad mood. But you can't be antagonistic or harassing in your behavior. Remember that the caller is likely viewing your comments. 2) No trying to figure out callers' identities. Any threads that try to investigate or reveal the identities of callers to the show will be removed and their authors will be as well. It goes against the spirit of the whole thing! Former callers are welcome to out themselves and/or ask a mod to post an update (though we will generally limit this to one post per former caller). 3) No Self Promotion. First time members are encouraged to become familiar with the group and join discussion. We will have occasional self promotion – mega threads, but not except posts between them! 4) New episodes should have discussion limited to the episode's 'comments thread' No one likes spoilers! If you have a comment about a specific episode, find its official episode thread. If you're not sure how to find the official thread, see #5. 5) Before posting, use the search bar to check for existing threads related to your topic. From the main page of the group, the search bar will be up top in mobile or to the left on your computer screen. Type in your key words and select the 'in group' option and relevant results will pop up Repeat posts (i.e. where is everyone from, what’s your favorite episode) will not be accepted. Nor will comments related to episodes. Find the existing thread first. 6. Please refrain from tagging Chris in your comments and posts. We promise, Chris does read this group and your tag will not change the likelihood of your message getting seen. If you have specific concerns of things happening in the groups please DM a mod. A list of mods can be found under the member's tab. 7. Keep posts related to the podcast. Off topic posts will often not be approved. For Gethard show content please see the “Gethhead” group. This goes for mental health related posts as well. Despite all the good work Chris has done on this front, we are not qualified to deal with those types of posts. Please see our mental health resources list”: https://docs.google.com/.../1luplyuqPYhkQ5ZuQ.../mobilebasic 8. Have fun and thank you for listening to B/A. - Chris Gethard and the Mods

                 Hello everyone, let me be the first to welcome you to Sailor Moon There are a few rules that need to be followed if you want to participate on Sailor Moon 1) Please make sure that whatever you post here is not offensive. If you have a problem, please contact or tag one of the admins and they will help you resolve your problem. You can view the admin list by selecting “members” and then choose to see your admin list. 2) No pornographic pictures will be allowed as per Facebook’s official site-wide rules. You will be removed if you post anything of that nature. 3) There is no rule #3. 4) Verbal harassment of other members will not be tolerated at all. Anyone found doing so will be given a warning 3 warnings and you will be removed. 5) This is a Sailor Moon fan group so please let your post reflect that. Only SM related content is allowed on our group. 6) No advertising of other groups will be permitted unless it is given the "OK" by the admins. Your post will be removed if not previously approved. 7) Do not role-play (RP) in a group discussion threads. 8) Do not block admins. If any one of us is not able to participate in your threads or view your posts, you will be automatically removed from the group.
